***богатеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатеть.html>богате́ть</a> (24019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bogátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатеть.html>богате́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bogatétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбогатеть.html>разбогате́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow rich</li></ol>

***богатый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a> (11107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">богатъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bogatŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bogatъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bogátyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:богач.html>бога́че</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатейший.html>богате́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rich, wealthy</li></ol>

***богатырь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богаты́рь</a> (9334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language, probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khazar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Khazar language">Khazar</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg/220px-Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg/330px-Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg/440px-Die_drei_Bogatyr.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2114" data-file-height="1400" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>«<a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>Богатыри́</a>» - Добрыня Никитич, Илья <a href = vnd.unilang:муромец.html>Му́ромец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Алёша Попович</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богаты́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bogatýrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богатыря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богатыри́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богатыре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bogatyr, a medieval Russian heroic warrior
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1831</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pushkin" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Pushkin">Alexander Pushkin</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:царь.html>царе́</a> салта́не</cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tale_of_Tsar_Saltan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tale of Tsar Saltan">The Tale of Tsar Saltan</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— "<a href = vnd.unilang:кабы.html>ка́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a>,— / <a href = vnd.unilang:третий.html>тре́тья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молвить.html>мо́лвила</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестрица.html>сестри́ца</a>,— / <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> б <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> ба́тюшки-царя́ / <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>родила́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:богатырь.html>богатыря́</a></b>".</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— "Káby já bylá caríca,— / Trétʹja mólvila sestríca,— / Ja b dlja bátjuški-carjá / Rodilá <b>bogatyrjá</b>".</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">But the youngest of the three / Murmured: "If he married me– / I would give our tsar <b>an heir</b> / <b>Handsome, brave, beyond compare</b>."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>strongly built man, hero</li></ol>

***богач.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:богач.html>бога́ч</a> (5985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bogačь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wealthy man</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bogъ</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ačь</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ач</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ač</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>rich man

***бодрить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бодрить.html>бодри́ть</a> (25280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрый.html>бо́дрый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bódryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрить.html>бодри́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bodrítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to stimulate, to invigorate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрить.html>бодри́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vózdux <b>bodrít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the air is bracing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бодрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бодрый.html>бо́дрый</a> (5739)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бъдръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bŭdrŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъdrъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alert, cheerful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bъděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be awake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-rъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрый.html>бо́дрый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bódryj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бодре́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бодре́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cheerful</li>
<li>brisk</li>
<li>sprightly</li>
<li>awake</li>
<li>vigorous, vivacious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодрить.html>бодри́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bodrítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***бодяга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бодяга.html>бодя́га</a> (28337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an unclear root + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́га</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jága</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодяга.html>бодя́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bodjága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодяга.html>бодя́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодяга.html>бодя́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бодяга.html>бодя́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> freshwater sponge</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> badyaga <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">folk medicine derived from the freshwater sponge, used for bruises</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> criminal slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diluted, surrogate or fake substance sold as the original, pure substance</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nonsense; long-winded chatter</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***боевик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боеви́к</a> (3848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bojevój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боеви́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bojevík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боевика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боевики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боевико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a militant, an insurgent, a fighter <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a member of an illegal armed group</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a fighter, a pugilist <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a person who engages in tussles and fistfights</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an action movie
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тех</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:боевик.html>боевико́в</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz tex <b>bojevikóv</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from those <b>action movie</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a blockbuster <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an exceptionally <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> movie or performance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inamimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a fighter plane
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истребитель.html>истреби́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">istrebítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***боевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́й</a> (1009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bojevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> combat, battle, fighting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bojevój</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>combat</b> formation, <b>battle</b> formation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bojevóje</b> iskússtvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">martial art</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>combat</b> art, <b>fighting</b> art</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> militant, bellicose, belligerent, active</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vojénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строевой.html>строево́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">strojevój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bojepripás</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́сов</a></b>)

<ol><li>explosive ordnance, weapon, shell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">неразорва́вшийся <b><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:означать.html>означа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взрывоопасный.html>взрывоопа́сный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́с</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инициированный.html>иниции́рован</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:снаряжённый.html>снаряжён</a>, взведён <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> ка́к-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовленный.html>пригото́влен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:применение.html>примене́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:применённый.html>применён</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вооруженный.html>вооружённом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конфликт.html>конфли́кте</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nerazorvávšijsja <b>bojepripás</b> označájet vzryvoopásnyj <b>bojepripás</b>, kotóryj byl iniciírovan, snarjažón, vzvedjón íli kák-libo ináče prigotóvlen k primenéniju i primenjón v vooružónnom konflíkte.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Unexploded <b>ordnance</b> means <b>explosive ordnance</b> that has been initiated, primed, fused or otherwise prepared for use and then used in armed conflict.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособность.html>боеспосо́бность</a> (25903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1894 [see citations]. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:способность.html>спосо́бность</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sposóbnostʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">capacity, power</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kampffähigkeit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособность.html>боеспосо́бность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bojesposóbnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособность.html>боеспосо́бности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособность.html>боеспосо́бности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боеспособность.html>боеспосо́бностей</a></b>)
